   if (lower.match(/help|how do|explain|tell me/)) return 'help';\\\\n    \\\\n    return 'general';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n of negative) {\\\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'negative';\\\\n    }\\\\n    \\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeEmotion(text) {\\\\n    const lower = \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|where/)) return 'query';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make/)) return 'create';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how|explain/)) return 'help';\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks|love|perfect/)) return 'positive';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate|terrible/)) return 'negative';\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\n    const r = {\\\\n        navigation: { positive: \\\\\\\"Taking you there!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Navigating now.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"On my way, boss!\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        query: { positive: \\\\\\\"Let me find that!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Searching...\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Looking it up...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        control: { positive: \\\\\\\"Done!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Stopped.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Action completed!\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        create: { positive: \\\\\\\"Creating now!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Making that...\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Building it...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        help: { positive: \\\\\\\"Happy to help!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Let me explain.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Here's how...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        general: { positive: \\\\\\\"Got it, boss!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Understood.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Processing...\\\\\\\" }\\\\n    };\\\\n    return r[intent]?.[sentiment] || r.general.neutral;\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n// 'SERVERCODE'\\\\\\\\n/**\\\\\\\\n * VISTAVIEW BACKEND v33.3\\\\\\\\n * Supports BOTH /api/xxx AND /xxx routes\\\\\\\\n */\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nconst express = require('express');\\\\\\\\nconst cors = require('cors');\\\\\\\\nconst { Pool } = require('pg');\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nconst app = express();\\\\\\\\nconst PORT = 1117;\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\napp.use(cors({ origin: '*', credentials: true }));\\\\\\\\napp.use(express.json());\\\\\\\\napp.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nconst pool = new Pool({ database: 'vistaview', host: 'localhost' });\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n// \\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\n// HELPERS\\\\\\\\n// \\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|where/)) return 'query';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make/)) return 'create';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how|explain/)) return 'help';\\\\\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks|love|perfect/)) return 'positive';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate|terrible/)) return 'negative';\\\\\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\\\\\n    const r = {\\\\\\\\n        navigation: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Taking you there!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Navigating now.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"On my way, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        query: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me find that!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Searching...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Looking it up...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        control: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Done!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Stopped.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Action completed!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        create: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Creating now!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Making that...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Building it...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        help: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Happy to help!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me explain.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Here's how...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        general: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Got it, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Understood.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Processing...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" }\\\\\\\\n    };\\\\\\\\n    return r[intent]?.[sentiment] || r.general.neutral;\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n// \\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\n// voiceHandler = async (req, res) => {\\\\\\\\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\\\\\\\\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n analyzeSentiment(inputText);\\\\n        \\\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, page_route, created_at)\\\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, NOW()) RETURNING id\\\\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, page_route]);\\\\n        \\\\n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_transcript, intent, confidence, created_at) VALUES ($1, $2, 0.85, NOW())`, [inputText, intent]); } catch {}\\\\n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen) VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW()) ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) DO UPDATE SET occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()`, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0,100), intent]); } catch {}\\\\n        try { await pool.query(`INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at) (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who/)) return 'query';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close/)) return 'control';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new/)) return 'create';\\\\\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks/)) return \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\napp.use(cors({\\\\n    origin: ['http://localhost:5180', 'http://localhost:5173', 'http://localhost:3000'],\\\\n    credentials: true\\\\n}));\\\\napp.use(express.json());\\\\napp.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));\\\\n\\\\n// Request logging\\\\napp.use((req, res, next) => {\\\\n    if (req.method !== 'GET' || req.path === '/api/health') {\\\\n        console.log(`[${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${req.method} ${req.path}`);\\\\n    }\\\\n    next();\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// DATABASE\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\nconst pool = new Pool({\\\\n    database: 'vistaview',\\\\n    host: 'localhost',\\\\n    max: 20,\\\\n    idleTimeoutMillis: 30000\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n// Test database connection\\\\npool.query('SELECT NOW()')\\\\n    .then(() => console.log('  \\\\u2705 Database connected'))\\\\n    .catch(err => console.error('  \\\\u274c Database error:', err.message));\\\\n\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// HELPER FUNCTIONS\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    \\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show|take me|redirect/)) return 'navigation';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look for|where|what is|who is/)) return 'query';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit|quit|end/)) return 'control';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make|build/)) return 'create';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/update|edit|change|modify/)) return 'update';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/delete|remove|clear/)) return 'delete';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how do|explain|tell me/)) return 'help';\\\\n    \\\\n    return 'general';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    \\\\n    const positive = ['great', 'good', 'awesome', 'thanks', 'thank you', 'love', 'excellent', 'perfect', 'amazing', 'wonderful'];\\\\n    const negative = ['bad', 'wrong', 'error', 'hate', 'terrible', 'awful', 'horrible', 'worst', 'sucks', 'broken'];\\\\n    \\\\n    for (const word of positive) {\\\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'positive';\\\\n    }\\\\n    for (const word of negative) {\\\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'negative';\\\\n    }\\\\n    \\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeEmotion(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    \\\\n    if (lower.match(/happy|joy|excited|yay|woohoo/)) return 'happy';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/sad|upset|disappointed|unfortunately/)) return 'sad';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/angry|frustrated|annoyed|damn|ugh/)) return 'frustrated';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/confused|lost|don't understand|what\\\\\\\\?/)) return 'confused';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/worried|concerned|nervous/)) return 'worried';\\\\n    \\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\n    const responses = {\\\\n        navigation: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Absolutely! Taking you there right now!\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"I'll navigate you there to help fix that.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Navigating there now, boss!\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        query: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Great question! Let me find that for you.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"Let me search for a solution.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Searching for that information...\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        control: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Done! Glad I could help!\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"Stopped. Let me know what you need.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Action completed, boss!\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        create: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Awesome! Creating that now!\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"I'll create that to help resolve this.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Creating that for you...\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        update: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Perfect! Updating now!\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"Updating to fix that issue.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Making those changes...\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        delete: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Removed! All clean now.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"Deleted. Hope that helps.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Removed successfully.\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        help: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Happy to help! Here's what I know...\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"Let me help you figure this out.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Here's how that works...\\\\\\\"\\\\n        },\\\\n        general: {\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\"Got it! I'm on it, boss!\\\\\\\",\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\"I understand. Let me help with that.\\\\\\\",\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\"Understood. Processing your request...\\\\\\\"\\\\n        }\\\\n    };\\\\n    \\\\n    return responses[intent]?.[sentiment] || responses.general.neutral;\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// ENDPOINTS\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n\\\\n// Health check\\\\napp.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {\\\\n    res.json({ \\\\n        status: 'ok', \\\\n        version: '33.2',\\\\n        timestamp: new Date().toISOString() \\\\n    });\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// VOICE COMMAND - Main voice input endpoint\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\napp.post('/api/voice/command', async (req, res) => {\\\\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\\\\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\\\\n    \\\\n    if (!inputText) {\\\\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No text provided' });\\\\n    }\\\\n    \\\\n    const startTime = Date.now();\\\\n    \\\\n    try {\\\\n        // Analyze\\\\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(inputText);\\\\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(inputText);\\\\n        const emotion = analyzeEmotion(inputText);\\\\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\\\\n        \\\\n        // Save to global_interaction_ledger\\\\n        const ledgerResult = await pool.query(`\\\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \\\\n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\\\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW())\\\\n            RETURNING id\\\\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathyScore, page_route]);\\\\n        \\\\n        const ledgerId = ledgerResult.rows[0].id;\\\\n        \\\\n        // Save to boss_voice_inputs\\\\n        try {\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\n                INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_transcript, intent, confidence, created_at)\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\n            `, [inputText, intent, 0.85]);\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* table may not exist */ }\\\\n        \\\\n        // Learn pattern\\\\n        try {\\\\n            const patternText = inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100);\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\\\\n                ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) \\\\n                DO UPDATE SET \\\\n                    occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1,\\\\n                    last_seen = NOW()\\\\n            `, [patternText, intent]);\\\\n        } catch (e) { \\\\n            // Try without conflict handling\\\\n            try {\\\\n                await pool.query(`\\\\n                    INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\\\\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\\\\n                `, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100), intent]);\\\\n            } catch (e2) { /* ignore */ }\\\\n        }\\\\n        \\\\n        // Add to realtime feed\\\\n        try {\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\n                INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at)\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\n            `, ['voice_command', JSON.stringify({ text: inputText, intent, sentiment }), user_type]);\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\\\n        \\\\n        // Generate response\\\\n        const responseText = generateResponse(intent, sentiment);\\\\n        \\\\n        // Log TTS response\\\\n        try {\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\n                INSERT INTO tts_responses (input_text, response_text, tone, created_at)\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\n            `, [inputText, responseText, sentiment === 'positive' ? 'enthusiastic' : 'friendly']);\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\\\n        \\\\n        const processingTime = Date.now() - startTime;\\\\n        \\\\n        console.log(`  [Voice] \\\\\\\"${inputText.substring(0, 40)}...\\\\\\\" \\\\u2192 ${intent} (${processingTime}ms)`);\\\\n        \\\\n        res.json({\\\\n            success: true,\\\\n            ledger_id: ledgerId,\\\\n            analysis: {\\\\n                intent,\\\\n                sentiment,\\\\n                emotion,\\\\n                empathyScore,\\\\n                confidence: 0.85\\\\n            },\\\\n            response: {\\\\n                text: responseText,\\\\n                tone: sentiment === 'positive' ? 'enthusiastic' : 'friendly',\\\\n                speak: true\\\\n            },\\\\n            processingTime\\\\n        });\\\\n        \\\\n    } catch (err) {\\\\n        console.error('  [Voice] Error:', err.message);\\\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\n// LEDGER LOG - Alternative/fallback endpoint\\\\n// \\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\u2550\\\\napp.post('/api/ledger/log', async (req, res) => {\\\\n    const { user_type = 'boss', raw_transcript, page_route = '/' } = req.body;\\\\n    \\\\n    if (!raw_transcript) {\\\\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No transcript provided' });\\\\n    }\\\\n    \\\\n    try {\\\\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(raw_transcript);\\\\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(raw_transcript);\\\\n        const emotion = analyzeEmotion(raw_transcript);\\\\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\\\\n        \\\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \\\\n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\\\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW())\\\\n            RETURNING id\\\\n        `, [user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathyScore, page_route]);\\\\n        \\\\n        const responseText = generateResponse(intent, sentiment);\\\\n        \\\\n        console.log(`  [Ledger] \\\\\\\"${raw_transcript.substring(0, 40)}...\\\\\\\" \\\\u2192 ${intent}`);\\\\n        \\\\n        res.json({\\\\n            success: true,\\\\n            ledger_id: result.rows[0].id,\\\\n            analysis: {\\\\n                sentiment,\\\\n                emotion,\\\\n                intent,\\\\n                empathyScore\\\\n            },\\\\n            tts_response: {\\\\n                text: responseText,\\\\n                tone: 'friendly'\\\\n            }\\\\n        });\\\\n        \\\\n    } catch (err) {\\\\n        console.error('  [Ledger] Error:', err.message);\\\\n        res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });\\\\n    }\\\\n});\\\\n\\\\n// status: 'learning'\\\\n        });\\\\n        \\\\n    } catch (err) {\\\\n        console.error('  [Stats] Error:', err.message);\\\\n        res.json({\\\\n            interactions: 0,\\\\n analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show|take me|redirect/)) return 'navigation';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look for|where|what is|who is/)) return 'query';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit|quit|end/)) return 'control';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make|build/)) return 'create';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/update|edit|change|modify/)) return 'update';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/delete|remove|clear/)) return 'delete';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how do|explain|tell me/)) return 'help';\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    const positive = ['great', 'good', 'awesome', 'thanks', 'thank you', 'love', 'excellent', 'perfect', 'amazing', 'wonderful'];\\\\\\\\n    const negative = ['bad', 'wrong', 'error', 'hate', 'terrible', 'awful', 'horrible', 'worst', 'sucks', 'broken'];\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    for (const word of positive) {\\\\\\\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'positive';\\\\\\\\n    }\\\\\\\\n    for (const word of negative) {\\\\\\\\n        if (lower.includes(word)) return 'negative';\\\\\\\\n    }\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeEmotion(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/happy|joy|excited|yay|woohoo/)) return 'happy';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/sad|upset|disappointed|unfortunately/)) return 'sad';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/angry|frustrated|annoyed|damn|ugh/)) return 'frustrated';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/confused|lost|don't understand|what\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\?/)) return 'confused';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/worried|concerned|nervous/)) return 'worried';\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\\\\\n    const responses = {\\\\\\\\n        navigation: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Absolutely! Taking you there right now!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"I'll navigate you there to help fix that.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Navigating there now, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        query: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Great question! Let me find that for you.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me search for a solution.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Searching for that information...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        control: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Done! Glad I could help!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Stopped. Let me know what you need.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Action completed, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        create: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Awesome! Creating that now!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"I'll create that to help resolve this.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Creating that for you...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        update: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Perfect! Updating now!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Updating to fix that issue.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Making those changes...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        delete: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Removed! All clean now.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Deleted. Hope that helps.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Removed successfully.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        help: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Happy to help! Here's what I know...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me help you figure this out.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Here's how that works...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        },\\\\\\\\n        general: {\\\\\\\\n            positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Got it! I'm on it, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"I understand. Let me help with that.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\",\\\\\\\\n            neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Understood. Processing your request...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n        }\\\\\\\\n    };\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    return responses[intent]?.[sentiment] || responses.general.neutral;\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n// \\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\n// VOICE COMMAND - Main voice input endpoint\\\\\\\\n// \\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\u2550\\\\\\\\napp.post('/api/voice/command', async (req, res) => {\\\\\\\\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\\\\\\\\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    if (!inputText) {\\\\\\\\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No text provided' });\\\\\\\\n    }\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    const startTime = Date.now();\\\\\\\\n    \\\\\\\\n    try {\\\\\\\\n        // Analyze\\\\\\\\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(inputText);\\\\\\\\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(inputText);\\\\\\\\n        const emotion = analyzeEmotion(inputText);\\\\\\\\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Save to global_interaction_ledger\\\\\\\\n        const ledgerResult = await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \\\\\\\\n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\\\\\\\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, $7, NOW())\\\\\\\\n            RETURNING id\\\\\\\\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, emotion, empathyScore, page_route]);\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        const ledgerId = ledgerResult.rows[0].id;\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Save to boss_voice_inputs\\\\\\\\n        try {\\\\\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n                INSERT INTO boss_voice_inputs (raw_transcript, intent, confidence, created_at)\\\\\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\\\\\n            `, [inputText, intent, 0.85]);\\\\\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* table may not exist */ }\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Learn pattern\\\\\\\\n        try {\\\\\\\\n            const patternText = inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100);\\\\\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\\\\\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\\\\\\\\n                ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) \\\\\\\\n                DO UPDATE SET \\\\\\\\n                    occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1,\\\\\\\\n                    last_seen = NOW()\\\\\\\\n            `, [patternText, intent]);\\\\\\\\n        } catch (e) { \\\\\\\\n            // Try without conflict handling\\\\\\\\n            try {\\\\\\\\n                await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n                    INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\\\\\\\\n                    VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\\\\\\\\n                `, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100), intent]);\\\\\\\\n            } catch (e2) { /* ignore */ }\\\\\\\\n        }\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Add to realtime feed\\\\\\\\n        try {\\\\\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n                INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at)\\\\\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\\\\\n            `, ['voice_command', JSON.stringify({ text: inputText, intent, sentiment }), user_type]);\\\\\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Generate response\\\\\\\\n        const responseText = generateResponse(intent, sentiment);\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Log TTS response\\\\\\\\n        try {\\\\\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\\\\\n                INSERT INTO tts_responses (input_text, response_text, tone, created_at)\\\\\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())\\\\\\\\n            `, [inputText, responseText, sentiment === 'positive' ? 'enthusiastic' : 'friendly']);\\\\\\\\n        } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        const processingTime = Date.now() - startTime;\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        console.log(`  [Voice] \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"${inputText.substring(0, 40)}...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" \\\\\\\\u2192 ${intent} (${processingTime}ms)`);\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        res.json({\\\\\\\\n            success: true,\\\\\\\\n            ledger_id: ledgerId,\\\\\\\\n            analysis: {\\\\\\\\n                intent,\\\\\\\\n                sentiment,\\\\\\\\n                emotion,\\\\\\\\n                empathyScore,\\\\\\\\n                confidence: 0.85\\\\\\\\n            },\\\\\\\\n            response: {\\\\\\\\n                text: responseText,\\\\\\\\n                tone: sentiment === 'positive' ? analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|where/)) return 'query';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make/)) return 'create';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how|explain/)) return 'help';\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks|love|perfect/)) return 'positive';\\\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate|terrible/)) return 'negative';\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\n    const r = {\\\\n        navigation: { positive: \\\\\\\"Taking you there!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Navigating now.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"On my way, boss!\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        query: { positive: \\\\\\\"Let me find that!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Searching...\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Looking it up...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        control: { positive: \\\\\\\"Done!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Stopped.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Action completed!\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        create: { positive: \\\\\\\"Creating now!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Making that...\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Building it...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        help: { positive: \\\\\\\"Happy to help!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Let me explain.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Here's how...\\\\\\\" },\\\\n        general: { positive: \\\\\\\"Got it, boss!\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\"Understood.\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\"Processing...\\\\\\\" }\\\\n    };\\\\n    return r[intent]?.[sentiment] || r.general.neutral;\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\n// voiceHandler = async (req, res) => {\\\\n    const { text, transcript, user_type = 'boss', page_route = '/' } = req.body;\\\\n    const inputText = text || transcript;\\\\n    \\\\n    if (!inputText) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No text' });\\\\n    \\\\n    try {\\\\n        const intent = analyzeIntent(inputText);\\\\n        const sentiment = analyzeSentiment(inputText);\\\\n        const empathyScore = sentiment === 'positive' ? 0.9 : sentiment === 'negative' ? 0.6 : 0.75;\\\\n        \\\\n        const result = await pool.query(`\\\\n            INSERT INTO global_interaction_ledger \\\\n            (user_type, raw_transcript, intent, sentiment, empathy_score, page_route, created_at)\\\\n            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6, NOW()) RETURNING id\\\\n        `, [user_type, inputText, intent, sentiment, empathyScore, page_route]);\\\\n        \\\\n        // Learn pattern\\\\n        try {\\\\n            await pool.query(`\\\\n                INSERT INTO learned_patterns (pattern_text, pattern_type, occurrence_count, last_seen)\\\\n                VALUES ($1, $2, 1, NOW())\\\\n                ON CONFLICT (pattern_text) DO UPDATE SET occurrence_count = learned_patterns.occurrence_count + 1, last_seen = NOW()\\\\n            `, [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100), intent]);\\\\n        } catch(e) {}\\\\n        \\\\n        // Feed\\\\n        try {\\\\n            await pool.query(`INSERT INTO realtime_feed (event_type, event_data, source, created_at) VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW())`,\\\\n                ['voice', JSON.stringify({text: inputText, intent}), user_type]);\\\\n        } catch(e) {}\\\\n        \\\\n        console.log(`[Voice] \\\\\\\"${inputText.substring(0,30)}...\\\\\\\" \\\\u2192 ${intent}`);\\\\n        \\\\n        res.json({\\\\n            success: true,\\\\n            ledger_id: result.rows[0].id,\\\\n            analysis: { intent, sentiment, empathyScore },\\\\n            response: { text: generateResponse(intent, sentiment), speak: true }\\\\n        });\\\\n    } catch (err) {\\\\n        console.error('[Voice] Error:', err.message);\\\\n analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who|where/)) return 'query';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close|exit/)) return 'control';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new|make/)) return 'create';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/help|how|explain/)) return 'help';\\\\\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks|love|perfect/)) return 'positive';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate|terrible/)) return 'negative';\\\\\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\\\\\n    const r = {\\\\\\\\n        navigation: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Taking you there!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Navigating now.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"On my way, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        query: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me find that!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Searching...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Looking it up...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        control: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Done!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Stopped.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Action completed!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        create: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Creating now!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Making that...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Building it...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        help: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Happy to help!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Let me explain.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Here's how...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" },\\\\\\\\n        general: { positive: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Got it, boss!\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", negative: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Understood.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\", neutral: \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Processing...\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" }\\\\\\\\n    };\\\\\\\\n    return r[intent]?.[sentiment] || r.general.neutral;\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n// [inputText.toLowerCase().substring(0, 100), intent]);\\\\\\\\n        } catch(e) {}\\\\\\\\n        \\\\\\\\n        // Feed\\\\\\\\n        try {\\\\\\\\n            await pool.query(`INSERT INTO res.json({\\\\\\\\n            success: true,\\\\\\\\n            ledger_id: result.rows[0].id,\\\\\\\\n            analysis: { intent, sentiment, empathyScore },\\\\\\\\n            response: { text: 'negative';\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\n}\\\\n\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\n    const r = {\\\\n        navigation: \\\\\\\"Taking you there, boss!\\\\\\\",\\\\n analyzeIntent(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/navigate|go to|open|show/)) return 'navigation';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/search|find|look|what|who/)) return 'query';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/stop|cancel|close/)) return 'control';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/create|add|new/)) return 'create';\\\\\\\\n    return 'general';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction analyzeSentiment(text) {\\\\\\\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/great|good|awesome|thanks/)) return 'positive';\\\\\\\\n    if (lower.match(/bad|wrong|error|hate/)) return 'negative';\\\\\\\\n    return 'neutral';\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nfunction generateResponse(intent, sentiment) {\\\\\\\\n };\\\\\\\\n    return r[intent] || r.general;\\\\\\\\n}\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\n//
